### [240] [FlowPipe: LLM-Enhanced Conditional Generative Flow Networks for Data Preparation Pipeline Construction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24679)
*Kunyu Ni,Lei Cao,Jie He,Xiaotong Zhang,Jianfeng Jin,Junyu Dong,Yanwei Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FlowPipe是一个基于条件生成流网络的统一框架，用于自动构建机器学习数据预处理管道，通过将管道合成建模为有向无环图上的条件概率流生成，显著提升了搜索效率和质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SOTA的Multi-DQN方法存在三个关键局限：解耦的值估计器削弱了长期信用分配、数据集上下文仅弱注入到策略中、在稀疏搜索空间中探索效率低下且存在许多无效状态。

Method: FlowPipe使用条件生成流网络（C-GFlowNets）结合轨迹平衡目标，通过深度语义调制（FiLM）引入LLM导出的逻辑先验，并将失败感知纳入流目标以避开无效状态。

Result: 在74个真实世界数据集的实验表明，FlowPipe平均提升准确率11.96%，训练收敛速度提高12.5倍。

Conclusion: FlowPipe通过统一框架有效解决了数据预处理管道自动构建中的组合优化难题，显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Data preparation pipelines improve data quality in machine learning by transforming raw tables into learning-ready data through sequential cleaning and feature transformation operators. However, automatically constructing such pipelines is computationally difficult because operator sequences are combinatorial and end-to-end evaluation is expensive. Existing state-of-the-art (SOTA) Multi-DQN methods still face three key limitations: decoupled value estimators weaken long-horizon credit assignment, dataset context is only weakly injected into the policy, and exploration is inefficient in a sparse search space with many invalid states. To address these issues, we propose FlowPipe, a unified framework that formulates pipeline synthesis as conditional probabilistic flow generation over a directed acyclic graph. FlowPipe uses Conditional Generative Flow Networks (C-GFlowNets) with a Trajectory Balance objective to connect terminal validation rewards with early pipeline decisions. It further introduces Deep Semantic Modulation through Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM), allowing LLM-derived logical priors to condition the policy's internal activations according to dataset semantics. In addition, FlowPipe incorporates failure awareness into the flow objective to avoid invalid states and concentrate search on high-potential regions. Experiments on two benchmark suites with 74 real-world datasets show that FlowPipe outperforms SOTA baselines, improving accuracy by 11.96% on average and achieving 12.5x faster training convergence. Source code is available at https://github.com/KunyuNi/FlowPipe.

</details>


### [241] [Grad Detect: Gradient-Based Hallucination Detection in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24790)
*Anand Kamat,Daniel Blake,Brent M. Werness*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Grad Detect，一种基于梯度分析的方法，通过在推理过程中进行单次前向-后向传播来检测 LLM 的幻觉现象，在多个基准测试中优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽然能力强大，但仍容易产生幻觉（hallucinations），在高风险应用中可靠部署 LLM 需要有效检测这些幻觉。

Method: 提出 Grad Detect 方法，通过分析推理过程中单次前向-后向传播的逐层梯度模式来预测幻觉，并发现最后五层集中了超过 97% 的判别性梯度信号。

Result: 在多个 Q&A 基准测试中，Grad Detect 在幻觉检测和模型弃权预测任务上均持续优于基于置信度和基于采样的基线方法。

Conclusion: Grad Detect 提供了一个统一的框架来预测 LLM 可靠性的多个维度，兼具强大的预测性能和可解释的模型故障定位能力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities across diverse tasks, yet they remain prone to generating hallucinations. Detecting these hallucinations is critical for deploying LLMs reliably in high-stakes applications. We present Grad Detect, a gradient-based approach for predicting hallucinations by analyzing layer-wise gradient patterns from a single forward-backward pass during inference. Our method shows that the internal gradient structure of a model carries rich information about the correctness of its output. This information is not accessible through output-level signals alone. We evaluate Grad Detect on several Q&A benchmarks across both hallucination detection and model abstention prediction, where it consistently outperforms confidence-based and sampling-based baselines. Through comprehensive layer ablation studies across all eleven models from four architectural families, we find that the final five layers concentrate over 97% of the discriminative gradient signal, enabling efficient deployment with minimal performance loss. Grad Detect provides a unified framework for predicting multiple dimensions of LLM reliability, offering strong predictive performance alongside interpretable insights into where and how model failures originate.

</details>


### [242] [Real vs. Complex Spectral Bases for Neural Operators: The Role of Green's Function Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24851)
*Jason Sulskis,Sathya Ravi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Hartley神经算子（HNO），作为Fourier神经算子（FNO）的纯实数版本，通过离散Hartley变换替代FFT，消除复数冗余。研究发现，HNO在自伴椭圆算子（如Poisson方程）上表现更优，而FNO在含相位的时间依赖算子（如波动方程、Navier-Stokes方程）上更优，并由Green函数理论给出了预测性规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FNO使用复数FFT处理实值PDE解存在表示冗余（共轭对称性），作者希望引入纯实数变换来消除冗余，并探究哪种谱基更适合不同类型算子。

Method: 将FNO中的FFT替换为纯实数离散Hartley变换（DHT），每个保留谱模式只学习一个实权重，无需复数运算；HNO与FNO等参数，仅在谱基上不同。

Result: 自伴椭圆算子（Poisson、biharmonic）上HNO优于FNO；含相位的时间依赖算子（波动、对流、Burgers、Navier-Stokes）上FNO优于HNO；热方程是边界情况。

Conclusion: 没有通用的最优算子，应匹配谱基与解算子的对称性：实数对称Green函数选HNO，含相位的算子选FNO。

Abstract: Fourier Neural Operators (FNO) learn solution operators of partial differential equations by parameterizing global convolutions in the complex Fourier domain. For real-valued PDE solutions, the complex FFT carries representational redundancy through conjugate symmetry. We introduce the Hartley Neural Operator (HNO), the exact real-valued mirror of FNO: it replaces the FFT with the purely real Discrete Hartley Transform and learns a single real multiplier per retained spectral mode, with no complex arithmetic. Because the real Hartley spectrum is not halved by conjugate symmetry, HNO retains twice as many frequency corners as FNO but one real weight where FNO carries a complex pair, so the two operators are iso-parametric at equal width and differ only in spectral basis. Our central thesis is that the best basis is a property of the operator. Self-adjoint elliptic operators (Poisson, biharmonic) have real, symmetric Green's functions that the real Hartley multiplier diagonalizes exactly, and HNO is favored there. Time-dependent operators carry phase, from oscillation in the wave equation to transport in advection, Burgers, and Navier-Stokes, which a real diagonal multiplier cannot represent, so FNO is favored there, and increasingly so with the operator's phase content, leaving the phaseless heat equation as the borderline case. Training both operators identically and benchmarking across PDE classes, initial-condition families, and boundary conditions, we find an elliptic-versus-time-dependent split that is monotone in operator phase content and matches the Green's-function theory we develop. Rather than a universal winner, our findings give a predictive rule: match the spectral basis to the symmetry of the solution operator.

</details>
